  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f91fc41b-04b9-4108-9329-b5a498d4043f'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText588158751217678275" style="display:none"><b>Johanna Walker is used to taking charge. But she’s about to meet someone who will make her lose control...</b><br /><br /> It has always been up to Johanna to care for her family, particularly her younger brother, Cole. With an absent father and a useless mother, she’s been making decisions based on what’s best for Cole for as long as she can remember. She even determines what men to date by how much they can provide for her brother and her, not on whatever sparks may—or may not—fly.<br /><br /> But with Cameron MacCabe, the attraction is undeniable. The sexy new bartender at work gives her butterflies every time she looks at him. And for once, Jo is tempted to put her needs first. Cam is just as obsessed with getting to know Jo, but her walls are too solid to let him get close enough to even try.<br /><br /> Then Cam moves into the flat below Jo’s, and their blistering connection becomes impossible to ignore. Especially since Cam is determined to uncover all of Jo’s secrets... even if it means taking apart her defenses piece by piece.</span>

<div id="review_609418147" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/609418147" />
    <a title="Baba  " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669232-baba"><img alt="Baba  " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564910043p2/4669232.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/609418147?book_show_action=true">May 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Baba  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Baba  " href="/user/show/4669232-baba">Baba  </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17280468-down-london-road">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=rolls-eyes">rolls-eyes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=dnf">dnf</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer609418147" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2340859620235323385"><b>2 stars**DNF at 60 %. I think my pic is more entertaining than the book.**Review posted May 10, 2013</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>As a side note<br/>My review of Down London Road is negative. Recently I have been accused of bullying for posting another negative review. Again, reading and reviewing is a very subjective matter. A review reflects my opinion. It reflects my feelings and it will always reflect why I enjoyed a book or why I didn't like it. Besides, I'm living in a democratic country and if I remember correctly then </i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText2340859620235323385" style="display:none"><b>2 stars**DNF at 60 %. I think my pic is more entertaining than the book.**Review posted May 10, 2013</b><br><br><b>
  <i>As a side note<br>My review of Down London Road is negative. Recently I have been accused of bullying for posting another negative review. Again, reading and reviewing is a very subjective matter. A review reflects my opinion. It reflects my feelings and it will always reflect why I enjoyed a book or why I didn't like it. Besides, I'm living in a democratic country and if I remember correctly then we're living and breathing our statutory right called "FREEDOM OF SPEECH". With that said, I would appreciate it immensely when those authors and readers who don't appreciate my take on a book would stop wasting their time by reading my reviews and posting vicious comments. Thank you.<br><br>Just to make this very clear: it was NOT Samantha Young who accused me of bullying, however, I wanted to add this side note to my review to point out that I have a right to express my honest opinion.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379791443i/550401._SY540_.png" alt=" photo Bildschirmfoto2013-04-19um234458_zps8bcced0f.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/550402.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lk8ypk2NlS1qaq59so1_500_zps51fdecff.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/550403.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mc6kyxFQBf1rwh77jo1_500_zps23144049.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jo's mother is unbelievable. Enough said. Maybe I could add that I'm going to dedicate a special shelf to...what's her name...? Can't even remember her name anymore. You can't blame me, though, because she is so forgettable. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/519023.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m6wvcp9NQv1rn19nco1_500_zpsf6fb3a32.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>**My review contains spoilers!**</b><br><br><br>I bought <i>Down London Road</i> on a whim and I must admit it was a mistake. The first 10 % of the plot were incredibly BORING. It picked up a bit but I never really got invested in the story. When I read...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You were a lot more loquacious last time we spoke."<br>Cam raised an eyebrow. "Loquacious? Does someone have a Word of the Day calendar?"<br><br>"A heads-up." Cam's deep voice washed over me. "So you're not too disappointed that Disney lied--no matter how much you wish it, I'll still be here when you open your eyes."<br>"I forgot to say condescending," I muttered unhappily. "Despicable, judgmental, self-righteous, obnoxious, condescending fuckwit."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>…I really thought we were on the right path. Was I ever wrong though.<br><br>Let's talk about inconsistencies. Our heroine is twenty-four years old, however, I wanted to yell at her to grow up already. She is responsible for her <i>wee</i> brother's well-being, she looks after him and does a fairly good job as far as I can judge, but at the same time she comes across as insecure, whiny, needy, and totally immature. She is even bad-mouthing herself. Can you believe it?<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"It's just part of being in a relationship with a guy who has money. I'm not good at many things, Joss. I'm not a scholar like Ellie or a writer like you. I'm a girlfriend. I'm a good girlfriend and my boyfriend likes to show his appreciation by being generous with his money."<br>(….)<br>"One: There's much more to you than that. Two: Do you realize you pretty much described yourself as a glorified whore?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Why she felt a sting of tears in her eyes is beyond me when she belittled herself all the time. Grow a pair already!<br><br>Riiiight. So, our heroine who has a major history of hooking up with rich men is not good at many things but she is a good girlfriend. Not a bit of it! The money issue bugged me. Granted, Malcolm didn't pay her bills but there's no getting round to state the fact that the money was on her mind. I felt it was some kind of golden parachute; the dough just kept lurking in a corner of her mind. Well, I guess you need to keep 'em warm, right? *rolls eyes*<br><br>I don't know why anyone would call his lover "boyfriend" if you are not in love with him. Let's be honest, I call that an occasional f@ck buddy. Come to think of it, she doesn't even spend the night with her "boyfriend" because after the deed is done she is leaving his flat to go home to her brother and mom. They tell each other <i>"I care about you."</i> Um…I care about my nice furniture as well. And I swear I really did care about my hamster when I was a kid. Sorry for being a tiny bit sarcastic, but there is a difference between caring for someone and loving someone. It was very obvious that she didn't love him and she didn't want him anymore. She was, however, way too chickenshit to address the issue.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420698ra/834839.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mf502rJ8dX1rosculo1_500_zps4dc3bca1.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I must admit the "mental" cheating was crap-tastic! Congrats, Jo, you outdid yourself! Seriously? The sex must have been very boring (or the man) when you need to think about another guy to get off. Can't remember that I've had another dude on my mind while in the throes of passion. Besides, she hasn't dumped her so-called boyfriend and yet she has no shame whatsoever to spend time and have fun with Cam. Plus, she was shamelessly lying to herself and to her friends all. The. Time. Does she not have any self-respect? PATHETIC. Of course that goes the other way round too. Right, Cam?<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>My own hand smoothed over my stomach, slipping under my pajamas and knickers so I could bring myself to climax, fantasizing about Cam screwing me against Su's desk.<br>I muffled my moan as I came and once the tremors stopped, I curled into my side, guilt cascading over me once again.<br>I was a terrible girlfriend.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I couldn't agree more!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>…I did the unthinkable. I closed my eyes and imagined Cam.<br>I came each time.<br>Malcolm took this to mean he and I were back on track and whatever had been bothering me before was dealt with.<br>I was an awful, awful person.<br>Yup. My world was full of color. Red for want. Yellow for shame. Green for jealousy.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I have to admit there are times when I truly feel ashamed to be a part of the female species when I have to make the acquaintance of women the likes of Jo. <br><br>Imagine, Jo is jealous of Becca. She'd rather mind her own bloody business! *shakes head disbelievingly*<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I coughed up the lie quite easily these days. "Of course. I'm with Malcolm. Why?"<br>(…)<br>"Because it definitely sounds like Cam's too busy shagging some noisy bird to want to have coffee with us."<br>My whole body froze as I stared at my brother, my heart pounding, a horribly uneasy feeling in my stomach as jealousy seized hold of me.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Friendly advice, Jo, if it's not to your liking anymore then call it quits. But. Please. Act. On. It. Don't wait until the situation is escalating. Stilted drama, anyone? Honestly, and then when they did split up (at 45 %) poor Malcolm--who I really liked up until that incident--told her he would be waiting for her when the other guy would dump her. He seriously told her he would take her back. WTF? Does he want to be her doormat? *serious headdesk moment* It's safe to say that my appreciation for Malcolm went down the drain at that very moment. He must have been incredibly desperate to articulate such nonsense. Uh-huh…dump him and jump the other guy's bones within…hmmm…how many minutes? Is this woman for real? She deserves a f@@@ing gold medal. And Jo should spare me her guilt trips. *insert major eye roll moment* <br><br>Shortly after, Jo and Malcolm happily exchanged texts in secret.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Cam cocked his head to the side. "Female logic. It needs its own decipher code."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I sure as hell need a decipher code to understand Jo.<br><br>The long legs and the hardening, tightening and pebbling nipples were all over the place. And let's not forget that bloody fake giggle. Repetitiveness, much?<br><br><b>What I liked</b><br><i>Be Caledonia.</i> That was lovely.<br><br><br>Overall the book was a huge disappointment. It provided too much stilted and forced drama, an extremely unlikable heroine, an even more extremely unlikable mother (yes, I need to borrow Lenore's gun) and the sex didn't do anything for me. At. All. Additionally I didn't feel their chemistry, the plot was mostly boring and the writing rather uninspiring. In conclusion, I'm going to return the book to Amazon for a refund because I didn't get my money's worth. I'm not willing anymore to pay Euro 8.52 for a bad ebook.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420698ra/834840.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m9wi5quTAk1qkulzco1_500_zps9cb97e98.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This might as well be another case of <i>"It's not the book, it's me."</i> Though it's safe to say it wasn't my cuppa. Just read it and I hope you'll end up enjoying it. Good luck!</span>
  <a data-text-id="2340859620235323385" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer453281296" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13406413724734267207"><b>10th November 2012</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s945.beta.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/library/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397235ra/766282.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>THERE IS MORE!!<br/>THERE IS MORE!!<br/>THERE IS MORE!!<br/>THERE IS MORE!!<br/>THERE IS MORE!!<br/>THERE IS MORE!!<br/>THERE IS MORE!!<br/><br/>MORE BRADEN! MORE MORE MORE MORE MORE MORE! <br/><br/>**Trying to push Brittany back into her hole***<br/><br/>When I saw On Dublin Street, #2<br/><br/><a href='http://s945.beta.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/library/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393653ra/757941.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://s945.beta.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/library/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397235ra/766283.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>9th January 2013</b><br/><br/>Soooooo I was just minding mah business, just chillaxin! Doing nothing really important.<br/><br/><a href='http://s945.beta.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_m19gzyofu41rs1ea8o1_400_zpsd2faa551.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397235ra/766284.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Then I receive a notification that someone liked me review of "Down London Road" and I am all...... WTF?!?!?! I aint read or wanting to</span>
  <span id="freeText13406413724734267207" style="display:none"><b>10th November 2012</b><br><br><a href="http://s945.beta.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/library/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397235ra/766282.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>THERE IS MORE!!<br>THERE IS MORE!!<br>THERE IS MORE!!<br>THERE IS MORE!!<br>THERE IS MORE!!<br>THERE IS MORE!!<br>THERE IS MORE!!<br><br>MORE BRADEN! MORE MORE MORE MORE MORE MORE! <br><br>**Trying to push Brittany back into her hole***<br><br>When I saw On Dublin Street, #2<br><br><a href="http://s945.beta.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/library/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393653ra/757941.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s945.beta.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/library/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397235ra/766283.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>9th January 2013</b><br><br>Soooooo I was just minding mah business, just chillaxin! Doing nothing really important.<br><br><a href="http://s945.beta.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_m19gzyofu41rs1ea8o1_400_zpsd2faa551.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397235ra/766284.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Then I receive a notification that someone liked me review of "Down London Road" and I am all...... WTF?!?!?! I aint read or wanting to read a Down London Road (clearly not knowing a title had been given!)<br><br><a href="http://s945.beta.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_m8em8voSFn1rs9q9ro1_r1_500_zps38949858.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397235ra/766285.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>So I have a look and I see not only does the 2nd installment have a title but also a BLURB!!!!!!!<br><br><a href="http://s945.beta.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_m69b36oTVR1rqfhi2o1_250_zps1c63be52.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397235ra/766286.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Now I was absolutely heartbroken that it was not a continuation of our Bray Bray.....<br><br><a href="http://s945.beta.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_m7ysefT5Zx1rwcc6bo1_400_zps5bd9eea7.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397235ra/766287.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But I don't doubt Samantha Young at all and I know she will captivate us as she did with On Dublin Street! I AM SO LOOKING FORWARD TO THE CHARACTERS MEETING FOR THE FIRST TIME! The Taxi scene was one of my all time best scenes for 2012! So I know this gotta be good!<br><br>Miss Young totally awesome!<br><br><a href="http://s945.beta.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_m8xib51xEz1rr2zps_zps2b9f259b.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380384772ra/743402.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And THEN I see release date for May 7th! <br><br><a href="http://s945.beta.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_m99h85iqqz1rcwzsbo1_500_zps7c320f46.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397235ra/766288.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>IT'S MAH BIRTHDAY! I think this will be the best birthday gift EVER!<br><br><a href="http://s945.beta.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_lvgkll3FwK1r6aoq4o1_400_zpseac837dd.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397235ra/766289.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>8th February 2013</b><br><br>WE HAVE A NEW COVER!<br><br><a href="http://s945.beta.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/New%20ones/16140408_zps35f5c43e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_453311737" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/453311737" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/453311737?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer453311737" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7163023234796349595"><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/4c88cba9-798a-46a2-b7d9-9441819903f9_zpsf3c37aa8.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397240i/766297._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo 4c88cba9-798a-46a2-b7d9-9441819903f9_zpsf3c37aa8.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>4.5 Stars!!!!</b><br/><br/>Okay. On Dublin Street was one of my favorites last year. Braden Carmichael is one of my top book boyfriends... I had really high expectations for this one. It wasn’t quite as good as ODS for me, but I still really enjoyed it! <br/><br/>In ODS we meet Jo. Jo is friends with Joss, they work together at the bar. On the outside, we see a good looking blonde, a gold digger who only dates rich men. <br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/a6655f56-a787-4ee0-8ccb-4341934060bb_zpsd86f6231.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397240i/766298.jpg' alt=' photo a6655f56-a787-4ee0-8ccb-4341934060bb_zpsd86f6231.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>But those that know the real Jo, the person on the inside know that is not the case. <br/><b>
  <i>
   </i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText7163023234796349595" style="display:none"><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/4c88cba9-798a-46a2-b7d9-9441819903f9_zpsf3c37aa8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397240i/766297._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 4c88cba9-798a-46a2-b7d9-9441819903f9_zpsf3c37aa8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>4.5 Stars!!!!</b><br><br>Okay. On Dublin Street was one of my favorites last year. Braden Carmichael is one of my top book boyfriends... I had really high expectations for this one. It wasn’t quite as good as ODS for me, but I still really enjoyed it! <br><br>In ODS we meet Jo. Jo is friends with Joss, they work together at the bar. On the outside, we see a good looking blonde, a gold digger who only dates rich men. <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/a6655f56-a787-4ee0-8ccb-4341934060bb_zpsd86f6231.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397240i/766298.jpg" alt=" photo a6655f56-a787-4ee0-8ccb-4341934060bb_zpsd86f6231.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But those that know the real Jo, the person on the inside know that is not the case. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“There’s so much more to you, Jo. How can you be happy to let people think these shitty things about you?”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Since Jo was a teen, she has been supporting her alcoholic mother, and her little brother. Cole means the world to her and she will do anything to make sure he is taken care of. She goes for guys that have money because she needs to feel secure. But she never dates anyone she isn’t attracted to, that she doesn’t at least care for. She works hard to provide for Cole, protect him. She doesn't only date rich men, she actually works to jobs. She wants things to be better for Cole, to make sure his life doesn’t turn out like hers. She loves Cole more than anything and he is the most important thing in her life. <br><b>
  <blockquote>I refused to ever let a day pass without him knowing how loved he was. Growing up, I’d never had that in my life and I was going to make damn sure that Cole did.</blockquote>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/daabe143-db50-406a-8bd8-d491a74bf29c_zps52b8616f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397240i/766299.jpg" alt=" photo daabe143-db50-406a-8bd8-d491a74bf29c_zps52b8616f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>One night Jo is out with her latest boyfriend, Malcolm. They are at an art showing of one of his ex’s. She see’s a guy there. This guy is sexy. He’s got tattoo’s, and beautiful blue eyes. The moment she meets his eyes, she feels a spark unlike anything she's ever felt. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/6fababa8-a4b2-427c-bf2b-55e6490e4be6_zpsf7309e0f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397240i/766300.jpg" alt=" photo 6fababa8-a4b2-427c-bf2b-55e6490e4be6_zpsf7309e0f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>My body was panting, "He's hot. Can we have him?" while my mind was screaming, "Oh, dear God, what the hell are you thinking?</blockquote>
</b><br>Jo knows her attraction to Cam is dangerous. He is not the type of guy she should be dating. And its obvious what he thinks of her. He see’s only whats on the outside. That she is an idiot, a gold digger. Nonetheless, Cam needs a job. Jo helps him out by getting him a gig bartending. While working together, they learn more about one another. Little by little, Cam starts to see the real Jo underneath it all. As luck would have it, Cam moves into a new apartment. That happens to be in the same building as Jo. He meets her brother and learns more about her situation. Things no one knows except Joss. He feels for Jo. He realizes how wrong he has been about her and sees that there is more to her than what meets the eye. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I've never met anyone as quietly brave and strong as you. I've never met a woman so unassuming, so kind, and so selfless. You are a complex lady." His mouth curled up at the corners. "And you are smart, and passionate, and funny, and exciting, and you blow me fucking away.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br> <a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/c055864b-4558-4969-8090-e247d0e43dd9_zpscca99763.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397240i/766301.jpg" alt=" photo c055864b-4558-4969-8090-e247d0e43dd9_zpscca99763.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After spending more time with one another, they become friends. Cam is a godsend to Jo. He connects with Cole. There is finally someone in her life she can lean on. Here is the rather frustrating part... I waited and waited for them to dump Becca/Malcolm. I mean, the feelings were there, and they were strong. There was obvious attraction... what was the hold up?!?! Eventually, they both come to the conclusion that they can’t be without one another. No matter what the consequences or lack of security, Jo has to make the decision to be with Cam. She is falling for him. And when they are finally together, it is worth the wait! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/c04af3f3-4877-4fc2-baff-fd0a36670c59_zps5c8dc4ac.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397240i/766302.jpg" alt=" photo c04af3f3-4877-4fc2-baff-fd0a36670c59_zps5c8dc4ac.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>For a while things are really good between the two of them. For the first time in Jo’s life, she has a partner. She is in a real relationship with someone she genuinely wants to be with. Cam wants Jo. All of her. He understands Cole comes first, and he is so good with him. But there are complications. Misunderstandings. Things fall apart for a while. Deep down Jo knows Cam is something special. <br><b>
  <blockquote>Cam wasn’t a perfect man- he’d proved that when we first met- but I was beginning to wonder if he might possibly be just a little bit perfect for me. Finally I’d found a guy who wanted to be with me- the real me.</blockquote>
</b> People make mistakes. There is some drama... but there is a hea :D<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/abe02281-f4d4-44d0-b906-e320aab0533a_zps29c14e74.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397240i/766303._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo abe02281-f4d4-44d0-b906-e320aab0533a_zps29c14e74.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I absolutely loved Cam and Jo together. Not only did I love the two main characters and the connection they shared, the supporting characters were just phenomenal! I fell in love with Jo’s little brother Cole. He was just awesome. And of course I love my Braden and Joss. Uncle Mick, Olivia, Ellie, Adam, Hannah, Nate, I mean there are just so many good characters! <br><b>
  <blockquote>“Some people are born with family, and others have to make family.” </blockquote>
</b><br>It has only been Jo and Cole for so long, it was beautiful watching her see that she really did have a family and people she could count on who cared for her. <br><br>Samantha Young’s writing is wonderful, and this story was emotional and beautiful. It was a story about learning to trust, open your heart and accept love.  <br>I’ve seen many mixed reviews on this one... A lot of my friends loved it, many DNF. I respect any and all opinions. I may be in the minority with loving this book... but I can’t help it I LOVED THIS BOOK! Was it as good as On Dublin Street... no, not quite... Did I love Cam and Jo as much as I loved Braden and Joss... again, no, not quite. But still a worthy 4.5-5 star read for me! One I really enjoyed and would definitely recommend! <br><br>And just because I love him so much... I am going to end this review on a high note, with my Braden Carmichael &lt;3<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/ce3371ab-5be9-41ec-aeb3-1429e712c000_zps785b2238.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397240i/766304.jpg" alt=" photo ce3371ab-5be9-41ec-aeb3-1429e712c000_zps785b2238.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="7163023234796349595" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_453944083" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/453944083" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/453944083?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101623503" href="/book/show/17280472-down-london-road">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer453944083" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9750897551649141529"><b>*2.5 Stars*</b><br/><br/>A largely uneventful read...<br/><br/>To be fair, I'll list some of my pros and cons:<br/><br/><b>
  <u>What I liked </u>
</b><br/>-Cole and Hanna were some of the coolest teens ever to grace a story!<br/>-The initial tension build up between Cam and Jo was fun.<br/>-Joss and Braden still being a strong part of story was awesome.<br/>-The strong sense of family and togetherness between friends was heartwarming. <br/><br/><b>
  <u>What didn't work for me</u>
</b><br/>-I understood Jo's insecurities, but her self-depreciation was over-the-top and didnt feel natural.<br/>-T</span>
  <span id="freeText9750897551649141529" style="display:none"><b>*2.5 Stars*</b><br><br>A largely uneventful read...<br><br>To be fair, I'll list some of my pros and cons:<br><br><b>
  <u>What I liked </u>
</b><br>-Cole and Hanna were some of the coolest teens ever to grace a story!<br>-The initial tension build up between Cam and Jo was fun.<br>-Joss and Braden still being a strong part of story was awesome.<br>-The strong sense of family and togetherness between friends was heartwarming. <br><br><b>
  <u>What didn't work for me</u>
</b><br>-I understood Jo's insecurities, but her self-depreciation was over-the-top and didnt feel natural.<br>-The book was dragged out with not much happening until the end, and by that point, I wasn't invested in the story.<br>-Hero and heroine weren't likable for me, and I never felt connected to either one. <br>-And finally, the plot itself and the story's occurrences just never genuinely interested me. <br><br>I really enjoyed On Dublin Street, but unfortunately did not end up loving this spinoff. I wasn't particularly fond of how Jo and Cam were portrayed, but I did adore many of the secondary characters and look forward to seeing how their stories evolve. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Contemporary Romance<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Extremely steamy<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Intense connection, but lacked believability.<br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Felt flat. Excellent secondary characters.<br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> Angsty and passionate, but uneventful. <br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Decent execution but did not pull me in. <br><b>▪ POV:</b> First person: Heroine<br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> None<br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412050368i/11316768.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Pretty-Words-Book-Blog/860331017317983" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height='“40"' width="150" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413062455i/11461733._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_458125690" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/458125690" />
    <a title="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12788865-rosalinda-krasnorada"><img alt="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583582487p2/12788865.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/458125690?book_show_action=true">Nov 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" href="/user/show/12788865-rosalinda-krasnorada">Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12788865-rosalinda-krasnorada?shelf=i-don-t-know">i-don-t-know</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12788865-rosalinda-krasnorada?shelf=abandoned">abandoned</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer458125690" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3080855226040944346"><br/><br/><b> ***PLEASE DO NOT READ THIS REVIEW IF YOU HAVEN'T READ THIS BOOK. SPOILERS AHEAD*** </b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397974i/768577._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I am very sorry, really really sorry because I wanted to LOVE this book but it didn't happen. I loved Samantha Young when I read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15760001.On_Dublin_Street__On_Dublin_Street___1_' title='On Dublin Street (On Dublin Street, #1) by Samantha Young' rel='nofollow noopener'>On Dublin Street</a> & <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17665083.Until_Fountain_Bridge__On_Dublin_Street___1_6_' title='Until Fountain Bridge (On Dublin Street, #1.6) by Samantha Young' rel='nofollow noopener'>Until Fountain Bridge</a>. They were WOW, amazing books, re-read worth it so I had expectations for this one... The thing is, in life you better have no expectations at all so you are not disappointed, right?<br/><br/>I must say I love Samantha's writing style and I will read more </span>
  <span id="freeText3080855226040944346" style="display:none"><br><br><b> ***PLEASE DO NOT READ THIS REVIEW IF YOU HAVEN'T READ THIS BOOK. SPOILERS AHEAD*** </b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397974i/768577._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am very sorry, really really sorry because I wanted to LOVE this book but it didn't happen. I loved Samantha Young when I read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15760001.On_Dublin_Street__On_Dublin_Street___1_" title="On Dublin Street (On Dublin Street, #1) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">On Dublin Street</a> &amp; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17665083.Until_Fountain_Bridge__On_Dublin_Street___1_6_" title="Until Fountain Bridge (On Dublin Street, #1.6) by Samantha Young" rel="nofollow noopener">Until Fountain Bridge</a>. They were WOW, amazing books, re-read worth it so I had expectations for this one... The thing is, in life you better have no expectations at all so you are not disappointed, right?<br><br>I must say I love Samantha's writing style and I will read more of her books, no doubt but I have to be honest and I cannot give this book a high rating because in my opinion and with all due respect, it does not deserve it.<br><br>This is the story of Jo &amp; Cam. We knew Jo from ODS. Ok, let's be honest. I didn't like her in ODS so I knew it was going to be hard to like her now but well, the author explains us the situations Jo has been through so you kinda understand her now. There's something I can't approve on her behavior and that's taking advantage of her "hotness" to attract guys with money. No! That has a name in my country and that's totally wrong, unless you want to do it professionally, I respect that. <br><br>I know she had a hard life and she's just trying to take care of her youngest brother Cole but you can get money working (she does it that way also) but taking advantage of rich men, that's a HELL NO for me.<br><br>Enter Cam, a hot tattooed guy. Jo sees him and feels an instant electricity, connection or whatever. Seriously? I need a plot, I need them to have feelings for a reason, not just because they're the hottest persons on the earth. I get it that they can feel attraction but that's it, don't try to sell me anything else in the first pages of the book because I can't buy it.<br><br>I will be back on my review after work today but these are my main issues:<br><br>*<b>The way she uses men</b> (even if she does it for a reason, I just don't care)<br><br>*Malcolm, I loved him but I wasn't suppose to love him, right?. <b>I just don't understand that they have been together for a few months but he's willing to wait for her after Cam breaks her heart</b>, seriously??? Is that happening in real life?<br><br>*The way she thinks she's not worth it BUT <b>when she refers to her she's the hottest thing ever </b>. Baby, chill out!<br><br>*Joss, yeah, the heroine in ODS. Are you telling me she was the same character??? I get she changed because of Ellie &amp; Braden but come on! I didn't recognize her at all, she was a new character for me.<br><br>*All the drama with her mum, you guys know I love drama but even this was way too much for me.<br><br>*Her <b>jealousy</b> about her ex-girlfriend from 10 years ago!!! OMG, noooo! <br><br>*Waking up after having sex and being with him 1 or 2 days and <b>being in love</b>! Don't try to sell me that because I just don't feel it.<br><br>*The story was very very very slow at the beginning, nothing happened in like AGES!<br><br>I also want to say a few good things about the book because the author deserves all my respect:<br><br>*<b>I loved the sex scenes</b> that I read. Samantha knows how to write sex scenes in my opinion.<br><br>*<b>I liked knowing about Braden/Jo &amp; Ellie/Adam</b>.<br><br>*I want to know more about <b>Hannah</b>, she's a smart ass but I love her anyway.<br><br>*I loved the moment when they almost kiss but she just stop it and he says:<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"So we're back to pretending there's nothing between us" </blockquote>
</b><br><br>I had goosebumps but it was the only time that it happened.<br><br>BTW, I am more than ok with cheating on books, I never had a problem (I loved Thoughtless so that says it all). What I didn't like about that was that she didn't leave Malcolm before because of his money but it wasn't the cheating what bothered me.<br><br>Also, and to be TOTALLY HONEST, if watching Issac Jones in action counts as mental cheating, I am guilty too!<br><br>FULL REVIEW TO COME ;)<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3080855226040944346" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer596999075" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7841595169781471482"><br/><b>*spoiler free - apart from a few direct quotes* </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1352.photobucket.com/albums/q659/Zippy1980/?action=view&current=1992c723d64ba090732dbc7c20a27b96_zps039a7b78.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>We first met Jo briefly "On Dublin Street", what I saw was a gorgeous, confident young woman but a gold digging, money grabber, who worked at Club 39 with Joss, and when she wasn't pulling pints she was basically trying to pull any rich bloke who could kit her out in all the latest fashions.......Well thats what I saw.........<br/><br/><b>What does Cameron MacCabe see? </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1352.photobucket.com/albums/q659/Zippy1980/?action=view&current=58757d1f025ba94f80969284ce30a185_zps948e336d.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>Cam....the sexy, hot, cocky tatt</span>
  <span id="freeText7841595169781471482" style="display:none"><br><b>*spoiler free - apart from a few direct quotes* </b><br><br><a href="http://s1352.photobucket.com/albums/q659/Zippy1980/?action=view&amp;current=1992c723d64ba090732dbc7c20a27b96_zps039a7b78.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418607i/829023._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>When you meet Johanna Walker, what will you see? </b><br><br><a href="http://s1352.photobucket.com/albums/q659/Zippy1980/?action=view&amp;current=f1264ba853aa69d3d23577337e670b1a_zps14aff638.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418607i/829024._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>We first met Jo briefly "On Dublin Street", what I saw was a gorgeous, confident young woman but a gold digging, money grabber, who worked at Club 39 with Joss, and when she wasn't pulling pints she was basically trying to pull any rich bloke who could kit her out in all the latest fashions.......Well thats what I saw.........<br><br><b>What does Cameron MacCabe see? </b><br><br><a href="http://s1352.photobucket.com/albums/q659/Zippy1980/?action=view&amp;current=58757d1f025ba94f80969284ce30a185_zps948e336d.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418607i/829025.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Cam....the sexy, hot, cocky tattooed guy, he's seen Jo's type before, the type that latches on to wealthy men, the type that use their bodies to get anything they wanted, the type with the annoying fake laugh and the fluttering eyelashes......<br><br><b>Well that's what Cam saw.......</b><br><br>But it's funny how in life you meet some people who build a mirage around them and if you really stop to look at them, if you really stop to peel back the layers, you'll find that what you thought you saw was really just an armour and underneath that armour is something else entirely. <br><br><a href="http://s1352.photobucket.com/albums/q659/Zippy1980/?action=view&amp;current=6c0dc3ed0722cf77fb1365c3f14f2982_zps2958bf6e.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418607i/829026._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So this story is about Cam peeling back Jo's layers, peeling back through her insecurities which are a result of the abuse she faced as a child, through her need to protect her 14 year old brother from their abusive, alcoholic mother, through her fear of not being able to provide for her family, fear of being hurt, of being left behind, fear of being her true self....<br><br><b>"You know, the world will always try to make you into who it wants you to be. People, time, events, they'll all try to carve away at you and make you think you don't know who you are. But it doesn't mater who they try to make you or what name they try to give you. If you stay true, you can chip off all their machinations and you're still you underneath it all." </b><br><br>This is one of those books that you pick up, you read the blurb, you think you know what you're getting but when you start to read you quickly see that you were wrong. So you keep reading and reading and all these emotions and memories hit you at once, suddenly real life fades into the back ground and it might be three in the morning but all you have to do is get to the end of this amazing story and as quickly as possible........ Yes this is one of those stories..... <br><br>This is Jo's story, a girl who's seen so much pain, a girl who will do what she has to do to protect the one she loves even if that means people never seeing the real Jo. In Jo's story, Samantha Young managed to make me experience nearly every possible emotion. Personally for me it was one of those books that brought such raw emotions to the fore front of my mind, I lived Jo's pain, when she was helpless, when she was anxious, when she felt worthless, when she was lost. But I was also there when she felt hope, when she felt strength, when she felt safe and when she felt loved.<br><br><b>"No one had ever told me I was smart or talented or brave, or that I deserved more than what I'd asked for." </b><br><br>After reading 'On Dublin Street' I was expecting to like this book, what I wasn't expecting was how much I was going to absolutely freaking love it. Right from the first chapter I loved learning everything there was to learn about Jo, the shadows that mark her past, her loyalty to her family, her determination to protect what is hers. I loved being immersed into her heartbreaking story, and watching as Cam tried to get under her skin.<br><br>As well as getting to know Jo I also loved reading more about the characters I fell in love with in "On Dublin Street". Joss, Braden, Ellie and Adam, Yes the team are all back, as well as some new characters who quickly endeared themselves to me. (Although there were a few who I wanted to throttle). <br><br>The writing was beautiful, Samantha Young is an amazing storyteller, who is able to breath life into her characters and really make you feel like you are their with them, rooting for their happily ever after. I was glued to the pages from the very first chapter, and OMG the sex scenes were amazingly erotic, in fact i'll be honest I was not expecting anywhere near the amount of steam this book delivers!!!!<br><br><a href="http://s1352.photobucket.com/albums/q659/Zippy1980/?action=view&amp;current=70436d149d880d6c56fb065ba9337c39_zps9f8272da.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418607i/829027._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>..... Definitely needed a cold shower at a few points in this book! <br><br>It's a beautiful, powerful and at times heart breaking, love story about seeing behind a persons armour, its about not judging a book by its cover, letting people in, taking chances and learning to trust. <br><br><a href="http://s1352.photobucket.com/albums/q659/Zippy1980/?action=view&amp;current=cdc00f70f96fc9167d09a85b702f0fa2_zps96d60223.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418607i/829028._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>5 amazing and well deserved stars, a book I would highly recommend. <br><br>Thanks to Netgalley and Penguin books UK for providing me with this amazing Arc in exchange for an honest review. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7841595169781471482" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1082394282" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1082394282" />
    <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu"><img alt="Ramona Popescu " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594649997p2/33526516.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1082394282?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ramona Popescu " href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu">Ramona Popescu </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=love-this-series">love-this-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=hot-romance">hot-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1082394282" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3760043851056827342">This series is really close to my heart, and each book has its unique story and characters. <br/>Having suffered and laughed with Joss and Braden, now we do it all again but with Jo and Cam.<br/>We know Jo from the first book, she is Joss's colleague and a good friend. Their relationship will go deeper in this book, and I enjoyed seeing the 2 of them together, so connected to each other and eager to help.<br/><br/>So, you all met Jo. She is smart, beautiful, caring, but with a bad background. She was abandoned by h</span>
  <span id="freeText3760043851056827342" style="display:none">This series is really close to my heart, and each book has its unique story and characters. <br>Having suffered and laughed with Joss and Braden, now we do it all again but with Jo and Cam.<br>We know Jo from the first book, she is Joss's colleague and a good friend. Their relationship will go deeper in this book, and I enjoyed seeing the 2 of them together, so connected to each other and eager to help.<br><br>So, you all met Jo. She is smart, beautiful, caring, but with a bad background. She was abandoned by her father, an abusive man, who in a way marked her forever. Her mother is an alcoholic, who was pretty useless, and Jo had to take care of her. She has a brother, Cole, who is her main focus in life. She will do anything to protect Cole and to guarantee him that he will have all the commodities he needs in order to study and become someone in life. Their relationship melt my heart. They love each other so much, are there for one another and the things Jo does are strictly for Cole, to be sure he doesn't suffer materially speaking. <br><br>Cole will be developed in one of Samantha's book and you will love the boy he became, all thanks to the protection his sister provided. Cam will also have a solid contribution, he will became a role model for Cole and will be a positive example in his development and career choice. Just wait and see. You will love their bromance. <br><br>In the name of this love, Jo was looking for older man who can provide her and her brother a certain material stability. She wasn't a gold digger, but she wanted that safety for her brother and to try to keep him safe, considering his background with their mother, who besides from being an alcoholic, was also abusive towards Cole. Jo consider that she didn't deserve to be happy and focused mainly on making Cole happy, encouraging him to study and now worry about who pays the bills and takes care of their mom.<br><br>Enters Cam.. the moment he met Jo, he was very judgmental and I kind of hate him for that. He only considered the exterior, and wasn't able to see Jo for the person she was: kind, caring and able to sacrifice anything for her brother. He was very mean to her, considering her a gold digger and making her feel kind of cheap because she was dating an older guy, Malcom, basely for his money.<br>The situation changes when Cam moved in Jo's and Cole building and they star to spend a lot of time together. <br><br>The first half of the book was a little boring for me, because I wanted the 2 of them to just realize how good they are together. The second part was interesting and very captivating. <br>After Cam realized what a jerk he was and saw the real Jo, he was mesmerized by her and we can't blame him, but sincerely speaking it took him long enough. He became determined to show her how wrong he was, how he made a mistake in making assumptions without knowing her and her circumstances. The spider scene was overwhelming.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1476453645i/20844195._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their romantic scenes were so hot and had Samantha's print all over them. The thing that I enjoy the most is her capacity of creating a new and better love story, with more passion and intensity, but giving each couple unique elements to define their relationship. You just don't read the same thing for 6 books, no.. you read an unique story, the only thing that binds them are the characters from the series.<br><br>Our old friends, Joss and Braden, are actively present in this book and you will love them even more. They had a definite contribution to our heroes evolution and you will see what true friendship means by reading this story.<br>5 stars for this book, besides the characters and the unique love story, it also generates a strong domestic message, but I will let you discover this by yourself.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479123324i/21149668._SX540_.png" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews please check <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com">https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="3760043851056827342" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_478138603" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/478138603" />
    <a title="Paula " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2879703-paula"><img alt="Paula " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1536687412p2/2879703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/478138603?book_show_action=true">Dec 15, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Paula " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Paula " href="/user/show/2879703-paula">Paula </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2879703-paula?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer478138603" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10968710392918131498"><br/>This is a damn good book. This story that made me laugh, cry, and smile. I always appreciate a well-developed friends-turn-lovers story. And one of the reasons I loved this book so much is that there was no insta-love crap going on here. Sure, there was an instant spark of attraction the first time Cam and Jo meet, but the romance between Jo and Cam is a slow yet sizzling burn. The sexual tension between these two could melt butter. <br/> <br/><i>
  <b>I’d never felt so intensely attracted to someone before. Us</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText10968710392918131498" style="display:none"><br />This is a damn good book. This story that made me laugh, cry, and smile. I always appreciate a well-developed friends-turn-lovers story. And one of the reasons I loved this book so much is that there was no insta-love crap going on here. Sure, there was an instant spark of attraction the first time Cam and Jo meet, but the romance between Jo and Cam is a slow yet sizzling burn. The sexual tension between these two could melt butter. <br /> <br /><i>
  <b>I’d never felt so intensely attracted to someone before. Usually, it took me a while to get to know a guy before I felt that kind of deep tingling in all of my good-for-nothing places.</b>
</i><br /><br />I really admire our misunderstood heroine. Jo’s a survivor, who is doing her best to keep from drowning in her struggles. And the way she protects and loves her little brother, Cole, when their parents failed miserably, is beautiful and courageous. But Jo has always been alone while dealing with her struggles. She never felt like she could be herself, always wearing a mask to hide who she is. And she’s never shared her issues with anyone. That is, until she met Cam, our hero, at a party one evening. Cam is exactly what Jo needs in her life - a lover, a friend, a companion, who understands and accepts everything about her. With Cam, she didn’t have to fake it, she could set herself free.<br /><br />There is something about a Scottish hero that makes me weak in the knees. Sigh. I love how passionate and protective Cam is. He’s also funny, sweet, and quick with the witty remarks. I had this sudden intense need to claim Cam for myself from the moment he walked onto the pages. And the fact that he’s just as beautiful on the inside as he is on the outside, only strengthens the adoring feelings I have for him. I love how honest and raw Cam is. He doesn’t let Jo run from him. He brings out the fire in Jo she’s always hidden underneath her mask. Cam makes her face everything head on. And, once he decided it was time to claim her, he made it very clear that he wanted all of her, or nothing at all. <br /><br />I absolutely adored Cam and Jo right from the start, even though they started off on the wrong foot. With any new romance, there will be problems and issues they will to work through. And there is definitely some drama, angst, and jealousy. This story is a little bit more serious and darker than the first book due to the topics addressed in this story. But, even with the bad, there is definitely a lot of good.<br /><br />I love the flirtatious, witty banter between Jo and Cam. They are so much fun. Have I mentioned how HOT they are together? Phew! Samantha Young definitely knows how to write wickedly sexy scenes that heat up the sheets. <br /> <br /><i>
  <b>“Cam,” I whispered, wanting him to pull away and needing him to never leave. He groaned and gently slid his forehead down the side of mine, his nose skimming my cheek, following my jaw, and coming to rest in a nuzzle against my throat. <br />I held my breath, waiting.<br />His hot lips touched the skin there. One brush. Two. <br />And then I felt the wet, hot erotic touch of tongue and I shuddered, falling against him.</b>
</i><br /><br />This book will leave an emotional impact on you and you will be wowed by the romance. There is no doubt in my mind that Samantha Young has become one of my favorite contemporary romance authors. I LOVE LOVE LOVE her writing. I have a feeling I know who the next couple is, and I’m very excited to read their story! <br /><br /><br /> <br /></span>

<div id="review_453997356" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer453997356" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13182921709563939444">Oh my stars!!! <b>Down London Road </b>was<i> sheer</i> perfection!! My heart is soaring after turning the last page!! It had <i> everything</i> I love and want in a romance, and <i> more</i>!! Longing , sexual tension, panty-melting scenes, sweet and tender love!! Family, friendship, and loyalty are all within the pages.<b>
  <i> I LOVED EVERY BIT!! </i>
</b>I probably should warn you, this review will contain gushing. Lots of gushing! <br/><br/>So it took me a minute to figure out who Johanna Walker was. Remember the gorgeous gold digger who wo</span>
  <span id="freeText13182921709563939444" style="display:none">Oh my stars!!! <b>Down London Road </b>was<i> sheer</i> perfection!! My heart is soaring after turning the last page!! It had <i> everything</i> I love and want in a romance, and <i> more</i>!! Longing , sexual tension, panty-melting scenes, sweet and tender love!! Family, friendship, and loyalty are all within the pages.<b>
  <i> I LOVED EVERY BIT!! </i>
</b>I probably should warn you, this review will contain gushing. Lots of gushing! <br /><br />So it took me a minute to figure out who Johanna Walker was. Remember the gorgeous gold digger who worked with Joss at Club 39? Yep, that’s her. But she’s not what we thought she was, and in the time between stories Joss has discovered this too, becoming an important and close friend. So, that’s a yes to anyone wondering if Joss and Braden show up in here: YES!! And quite a lot, and it was lovely!! <br /><br />Anyways, back to the story. Jo does have the reputation of dating men who have a lot of money. She’s not a gold digger per se, but she wants to find someone who will provide security for her and her fourteen year old brother, Cole. For years Jo has been the sole provider for their family, their mother being a raging, non-functioning drunk. She only pokes her head out of the bedroom if she comes up short on gin or to mutter a well placed verbal stab to Jo or Cole. However bad her mother is, her father was a hundred times worse. Thankfully, he’s out of their lives but not before inflicting serious damage to Johanna’s self-esteem. So, Jo does date nice rich men, and she masks her true personality to make sure she’s the perfect girlfriend. <br /><br />Enter Cam; he appears to be the opposite of safe. He’s good-looking, tattooed; cocky with an attitude. He has lust in his eyes for Johanna when he first sees her, then contempt when he sees her with Malcolm, her boyfriend. He assumes she’s just into Malcolm for his money and tells her so, getting off on a very bad foot. However, Jo does care for Malcolm, and he is everything Jo feels she needs to have a happy and secure future. So, she ignores her immediate physical attraction to Cam, and stays with Malcolm. This becomes increasingly hard when Cam starts work as a bartender for Club 39 with Jo and Joss. <br /><br />You know where this is going. Let me assure those out there, like me, who detest cheating stories. This isn’t one of them. What we do get is a friendship formed between Cam and Jo that builds into a <i> slow, hot, burning </i> desire! The hottest relationships start with the mind and emotions, and then turn into more!! They are my favorite type of romance to read about, and I LOVED this one!! <br /><b>
  <i><br />“Cam,” I whispered, wanting him to pull away and needing him to never leave. He groaned and gently slid his forehead down the side of mine, his nose skimming my cheek, following my jaw, and coming to rest in a nuzzle against my throat. <br />I held my breath, waiting.<br />His hot lips touched the skin there. One brush. Two. <br />And then I felt the wet, hot erotic touch of tongue and I shuddered, falling against him.<br /></i>
</b><br />Oh, the delicious buildup!! <br /><br />Did I mention the HOT factor? Any who read<b> On Dublin Street</b> knows that Samantha Young can write scenes that could make you spontaneously combust!! There really should be a safety warning: READ BY OPEN FREEZER. <br /><br />This romance is not without some angst, and exciting drama. Cam and Jo are involved with other people when they first meet, so this is not an easy breezy road, at first. Plus, Jo’s insecurities plague on her mind which are not helped by an old girlfriend popping up! There were a few scenes that made me gasp from stabbing hurt I felt for Jo!! But for the majority of this story, I wore a stupid blissful grin. *happy, happy, sigh*<br /><br />And now I get to the WORST part: I finished the story and now I have to wait for Samantha to write another!!!! *sobs*<br /><br />One of my favorite quotes: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <br />
  <b>
    <i><br />And I knew then as I was lying on our bed staring up into his familiar and handsome face that I had something I’d never had before. I had someone who wasn’t going to let me spend a single day of my life without knowing how much I was loved.<br /></i>
  </b>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><i> A copy was provided by NAL publishing in exchange for an honest review. Thank you!! </i><br /></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
